************************************************************

output is based on am implementation on additional inequalities.  Earlier, the equalities were not considered. In this case,
if there exist an equality of the form abs(ui-uj)=0 and an inequality of the form uk>ui, then in this implementation an inequality of the form uk>uj is added along with the existing to uk>ui.

The penalty functions is :

Invariant x>=y
If violation i.e.  x<y, then
temp= (float(x+1)/float(y+1+x+1))
penalty= (float(-1*(x+1))* math.log(temp))
